Sensor! pairs! 344! and! 748! were! the! most! important! sensors! pairs! in! the! non4destructive! evaluation!of!beam!HS4L4M41,!as!they!monitored!the!initiation!of!the!shear!crack.!The!Load4 HMI!graphs!for!these!sensor!pairs!are!presented!in!Figure!6.18c.!The!initiation!of!the!shear! cracks!was!visually!observed!at!the!load!step!of!300!kN!for!the!left!half!of!beam!HS4L4M41,! and! at! 250! kN! for! the! right! half.! From! the! Load4HMI! graph,! the! surface! opening! cracks! yielded!HMI!values!of!0.75,!and!0.51!for!the!left!and!right!halves!of!the!beam!respectively.! The!HMI!values,!although!quite!different,!are!both!indicative!of!a!cracked!section.!Using!the! 0.5!threshold!established!from!the!small4scale!experimental!program,!as!the!primary!source! to!evaluate!the!member's!condition,!the!left!half!of!the!beam!would!have!been!considered! cracked!at!the!225!kN!load!step,!and!the!right!half!would!have!been!considered!crack!at!the! 250! kN! load! step,! both! providing! a! warning! of! a! possible! future! failure! at! much! earlier! stages!than!conventional!means.!! The! Load4HMI! graphs! obtained! from! these! sensor! pairs! are! shown! in! Figure! 6.18b! The! section! monitored! by! sensor! pair! 243! was! found! to! have! two! cracks! initiate! through! the! signal! paths! at! load! steps! of! 225! kN,! and! 300! kN! yielding! HMI! values! of! 0.79,! and! 0.87,! respectively.!The!opposing!side!of!the!beam!monitored!by!sensor!pair!849!was!observed!to! crack! at! 175! kN,! 225! kN,! and! 300! kN,! yielding! HMIs! of! 0.68,! 0.72,! and! 0.78,! respectively.! Similar! to! the! results! described! from! sensor! pair! 344,! the! HMI! values! for! sensor! pair! 243! crosses!the!0.5!threshold!at!a!load!of!175!kN,!and!would!suggest!that!the!beam's!cracking! load! was! in! fact! 175! kN,! not! the! visually! observed! 225! kN! at! this! section.! Sensor! pair! 849! exceeded!the!0.5!thresholds!at!a!load!of!150!kN.!Both!sensor!pairs,!monitoring!the!initiation! of!cracking!in!the!effective!shear!zone!providing!warning!for!the!initiation!of!the!shear!crack! 25450!kN!prior!to!the!crack!being!visible!on!the!exterior!of!the!beam.!The!remaining!sensor! pairs!demonstrated!that!the!piezo4system!is!effective!for!the!detection!of!shear!cracking!in! a!reinforced!concrete!member.! Sensor! pairs! 142,! and! 9410! monitored! the! sections! of! the! beam! directly! adjacent! to! the! support.! Since! beam! HS4L4M41! was! designed! to! fail! in! shear,! due! to! its! lack! of! adequate! shear!reinforcement,!the!region!above!the!supports!was!expected!to!crack!once!the!shear! capacity!of!the!concrete!section!was!exceeded.!Although!no!cracking!was!observed!visually! 128!

between!sensor!9!and!10,!the!Load4HMI!graph!in!Figure!6.18a!demonstrates!that!the!beam! cracked! at! a! load! of! 525! kN.! This! result! agrees! with! the! calculated! failure! load! of! 530! kN.! Sensor!pair!142!demonstrated!similar!results.!As!the!beams!ultimate!capacity!was!reached,! two! cracks! appeared! near! the! left! support! of! the! beam.! The! first! crack! was! observed! to! cross!sensor!2!at!the!400!kN!load!step!and!yield!an!HMI!value!of!0.70,!and!the!secondary! crack!was!observed!to!intersect!the!signal!path!of!the!sensor!pair!at!550!kN!yielding!an!HMI! value!of!0.83.!Based!on!the!results!of!the!piezo4sensors,!the!HMI!value!for!sensor!pair!142! exceeded!the!0.5!cracking!limit!at!a!load!of!325!kN,!suggesting!this!to!be!the!cracking!load! for!this!signal!path.! The!results!obtained!from!the!sensor!pairs!monitoring!the!compression!zone,!445,!and!647! are!provided!in!Figure!6.18d.!Here!sensor!pair!647!exceeds!an!HMI!of!0.5!at!525!kN.!Since! sensor!pairs,!9410!and!647!exceeded!the!0.5!thresholds,!the!results!suggest!that!the!member! cracked!internally!beside!the!right!support!resulting!in!a!shear!failure.!The!results!between! sensors!pair!142!yielded!different!results.!A!surface!opening!crack!was!observed!at!a!load!of! 400!kN!yielding!a!HMI!value!of!0.71.!The!results!obtained!by!the!HMI!values!both!suggest! that! the! shear! crack! did! not! cause! concrete! crushing! between! sensors! 445,! and! the! crack! between!sensor!pair!142!was!captured!at!the!325!kN!load!step.!The!results!provide!that!the! system! is! effective! for! predicting,! and! capturing! the! initiation! of! shear! cracking,! and! providing!a!means!of!predicting!a!beam's!shear!failure!!

6.5.1.3 FBG,Fiber,Optic,Sensors, A!total!of!5!fiber!optic!sensors!were!installed!in!beam!HS4L4M41.!The!sensors!were!intended! to!monitor!the!shear!crack,!quarter4span,!and!mid4span!location!of!the!beam.!The!results!of! these! sensors! were! intended! to! provide! a! comparison! between! the! crack! widths! measurements! provided! by! the! piezo4system! using! the! proposed! HMI4Crack! Width! relationship,! and! the! direct! measurements! of! crack! width! provided! by! the! fiber! optic! sensors.! The! five! fiber! optic! sensors! were! multiplexed! into! one! continuous! cable.! The! continuous! cable! was! easily! installed! into! the! concrete! matrix! as! to! monitor! the! desired!

129!

locations,! although! due! to! the! fragility! of! the! cable,! only! one! of! the! five! sensors! worked! following!the!casting!process.!Since!the!cable!was!multiplexed,!when!the!cable!is!ripped!in! any!one!specific!location,!the!sensors!following!the!damaged!location!will!not!function.!The! sensor!installed!in!beam!HS4L4M41!was!torn!after!the!first!fiber!optic!sensor,!and!thus!the! remaining!sensors!did!not!work.!Figure!6.19a!shows!the!location!of!the!working!FBG!sensor.! The! FBG! sensor! monitored! the! concrete! strain! experienced! perpendicular! to! the! shear! crack.!The!Load4Strain!graph!is!presented!in!Figure!6.19b.!!

6.5.1.4 Crack,Width,Measurements,Using,Piezo`System,and,Member,Cracking,Behavior,, The! small4scale! experimental! program! helped! develop! a! universal! HMI4Crack! Width! equation! that! can! be! used! in! the! investigation! of! beam! HS4L4M41! to! quantify! the! appearance!of!cracking!in!terms!of!an!estimated!crack!width.!The!following!investigation!is! carried!out!in!order!to!check!the!validity!of!the!model,!and!to!demonstrate!the!abilities!of! the! piezo4system.! The! focus! of! the! HS4L4M41! experimental! program! was! to! predict,! and! detect,!the!shear!crack!of!a!reinforced!concrete!beam.!The!HMI!results!obtained!from!the! piezo4sensors!demonstrated!the!system's!ability!to!predict!and!detect!the!appearance!of!a! shear!crack.!The!system!is!required!to!quantify!the!damage!detected!in!terms!that!could!be! easily!interpreted!such!as!a!measure!of!crack!width.!The!HMI!results!obtained!from!the!six! sensor! pairs! monitoring! the! tensile! strains! were! converted! to! the! equivalent! crack! widths! using!Equation!6.4.!As!the!compressive!strains!were!not!yet!investigated,!and!a!model!was! not! developed! to! interpret! the! results,! sensor! pairs! 445! and! 647! are! not! part! of! this! investigation.! The! results! of! the! FBG! fiber! optic! sensors! are! converted! to! values! of! crack! width,!using!its!specified!300!mm!gauge!length.! The! crack! width! measurements! provided! of! the! fiber! optic! cable,! along! with! the! results! obtained!from!the!equivalent!piezo4sensor!pairs!are!presented!in!Figure!6.20a.!Figure!6.20b,! and! Figure! 6.20c,! show! the! cracking! behavior! of! beam! HS4L4M41! around! the! location! of! signal!paths!344!and!748.!The!crack!width!measurements!provided!by!the!fiber!optic!sensor! found!in!beam!HS4L4M41!is!expected!to!provide!results!agreeing!with!those!obtained!from! the! 748! signal! paths.! From! the! graph! obtained! in! Figure! 6.20a! along! with! the! cracking! behavior!in!Figure!6.20c,!the!results!of!the!piezo4sensor!agree!with!the!ones!obtained!from!

6.5.1.5 Results,Obtained,Using,the,MIRA,3D,Tomographer,, The!MIRA!3D!tomographer!was!used!to!map!the!location!of!cracking!within!beam!HS4L4M41.! Readings!were!taken!using!the!equipment!along!the!length!of!the!beam!as!well!as!along!the! height.!As!the!member!is!expected!to!behave!relatively!similar!on!both!halves,!only!half!the! beam!was!scanned,!and!the!results!are!presented!here!in.!Along!with!mapping!the!location! of! cracking! in! the! member,! the! MIRA! was! also! used! to! determine! the! location! of! steel! reinforcement.!Reading!were!taken!prior!to!the!member!being!loaded,!and!after!the!loading! program! was! complete,! to! provide! a! differentiation! between! the! healthy! and! damaged! state!of!the!member.! 6.5.2 HS-L-M-2 Beam! HS4L4M42! was! designed! to! fail! in! flexure! and! was! provided! with! the! required! shear! reinforcement!depicted!by!the!code.!The!beam!was!provided!with!more!than!the!minimum! stirrups!required,!as!to!guarantee!the!desired!flexural!behavior!of!the!member.!The!design! requirements!for!beam!HS4L4M42!would!aid!in!the!investigation!of!the!piezo4sensors!under! normal!working!conditions.!The!results!for!the!piezo4sensors,!installed!in!this!member,!were! processed!in!terms!of!the!strain!experienced!at!certain!locations,!along!with!the!crack4width! once!the!member!had!cracked.!A!total!of!ten!piezo4sensors!were!installed!in!beam!HS4L4M4 2,!with!the!primary!focus!of!investigating!the!flexural!behavior!of!the!beam.!A!total!of!seven! signal! paths! were! employed! to! monitor! the! flexural! behavior! of! beam! HS4L4M42.! These! seven! signal! paths! monitored! the! entire! clear! span! of! the! beam! near! the! tension! reinforcement.! An! additional! two! signal! paths! were! chosen! to! monitor! the! initiation! of! shear!cracking!in!the!member.! A!five!sensor!multiplexed!FBG!fiber!optic!sensor!was!embedded!into!the!beam's!matrix!for! monitoring! the! strains! at! predetermined! locations.! Two! sensors! were! installed! at! the! expected!shear!crack!locations,!beside!the!right!and!left!supports,!and!three!sensors!were! installed!at!the!quarter4span!and!mid4span.!The!fiber!optic!cables!provided!a!comparison!to! the! results! of! the! piezo4system,! and! provided! a! means! of! verifying! the! piezo4system's! functionality.! The! results! of! the! piezo4sensors! were! then! analyzed! for! a! means! of! determining! the! various! design! limit! states,! as! to! quantify! the! severity! of! the! damage! experienced!in!terms!of!the!code's!previsions.!

6.5.2.2 Piezo`Sensors,Location,and,Results, The! ten! piezo4sensors! in! beam! HS4L4M42! were! arranged! as! to! monitor! the! initiation! of! flexural! cracking,! along! the! tension! reinforcement.! The! piezo4sensors'! spatial! position! is! presented! in! Figure! 6.28.! Sensors! 1! through! 8! monitored! the! tension! side! of! the! beam;! while! sensors! 9! and! 10! were! used! for! shear! crack! detection.! The! location! of! the! piezo4 sensors! is! symmetric! for! the! right! and! left! halves! of! the! beam,! with! the! exception! of! the! shear!cracks!detection!signal!paths.!Sensor!path!943!is!located!800!mm!from!the!left!support! while! sensor! pair! 1046! is! located! 1000! mm! from! the! right! support.! The! lack! of! symmetry! between! sensor! pairs! 943! and! 1046! would! ensure! the! detection! of! the! shear! crack's! propagation.!Along!with!ensuring!the!detection!of!the!shear!crack!propagation,!asymmetric! characteristic! of! the! piezo4sensors! also! allowed! for! the! study! of! varying! sensor4to4sensor! distances,! as! to! establish! the! largest! sensor! separation! whiles! maintaining! the! system's! reliability.! As!in!the!investigation!carried!out!for!beam!HS4L4M41,!sensor!pairs!142!and!748!monitored! the!location!near!the!support!location.!The!regions!are!not!expected!to!exhibit!any!signs!of! cracking,! and! thus,! the! sensors! act! as! a! control! for! the! experiment,! verifying! the! cracking! threshold!for!the!HMI.!The!combination!of!adjacent!sensor!pairs!from!sensor!1!through!8! would!monitor!the!initiation!of!cracking!along!the!tension!face!of!the!beam,!and!will!be!the! primary!focus!of!the!study.!A!total!of!nine!signal!paths!were!studied!in!the!investigation!of! beam!HS4L4M42,!and!are!discussed!here!in.!!

Sensor! pair! 445! monitored! the! mid! span! of! beam! HS4L4M42,! the! Load4HMI! graph! for! this! sensor! pair! is! presented! in! Figure! 6.29d.! Since! the! mid4section! of! the! beam! would! experience!the!highest!moment!during!the!loading!procedure,!this!location!was!expected!to! be!the!first!to!exhibit!cracking.!From!the!visual!inspection!of!the!member,!a!total!of!three! cracks! were! observed! to! initiate! through! the! signal! path! of! the! sensor! pair! at! a! load! of!!!!!! 150!kN,!yielding!a!HMI!output!of!0.74.!This!large!spike!in!the!HMI!value!is!characteristic!of! the!initiation!of!cracking!through!the!signal!path.!Although!the!HMI!output,!would!suggest! that!the!member!initiate!cracking!at!a!load!of!125!kN.!! Sensor! pairs! 344! and! 546! monitored! the! sections! adjacent! to! the! midsection! of! the! beam.! The!results!of!the!two!sensor!pairs!are!provided!in!Figure!6.29c.!The!initiation!of!cracking! was!visually!observed!at!three!load!steps!between!sensors!3!and!5.!The!175!kN,!200!kN,!and! 250!kN!load!steps!exhibited!signs!of!cracking,!and!had!a!HMI!value!of!0.55,!0.64,!and!0.71,! respectively.!The!equivalent!section!between!sensors!5!and!6!exhibited!cracking!at!two!load! steps.!The!beam!was!observed!to!crack!at!the!150!kN,!and!200!kN!load!steps,!having!HMIs! of!0.52,!and!0.71,!respectively.!Based!on!the!results!obtained,!the!piezo4sensors!are!seen!to! yield!similar!results!on!both!ends!of!a!symmetric!beam.!Although!the!HMIs!at!the!cracking! loads! are! very! similar! for! both! sensor! pairs,! the! section! between! sensor! pair! 546! exhibits! more!distress!based!on!the!HMI!output.!As!the!load!is!increased!beyond!the!cracking!limit,! the!value!of!the!HMI!between!sensors!5!and!6!becomes!much!greater!than!in!the!section! monitored!by!sensor!pair!344.!Since!the!reflection!and!refraction!of!mechanical!stress!waves! is!largely!governed!by!the!width!of!the!imperfection,!or!crack,!intersecting!the!transmission,! the! results! suggest! that! the! combined! crack! width! experienced! in! the! section! between! sensors!5!and!6!is!slightly!larger!than!the!one!between!sensors!3!and!4.!!! Sensor!pairs!243,!and!647!monitored!the!sections!at!the!quarter!spans!of!the!beam.!These! sections!are!expected!to!crack!at!a!much!later!stage!in!the!loading!program!and!should!be! reflected!by!the!HMI!results!in!Figure!6.29b.!Surface!opening!cracks!were!observed!at!two! load!steps!between!sensor!pair!243.!Cracking!between!this!sensor!pair!was!observed!at!the! 325!kN!and!475!kN!load!steps,!yielding!HMIs!values!of!0.68,!and!0.76,!respectively.!Although! it!should!be!noted!that!the!HMI!value!for!this!section!was!very!small!up!to!the!275!kN!load! 145!

step,! as! not! much! damage! was! incurred,! after! which! the! HMI! is! seen! to! increase! tremendously!as!the!cracking!load!is!reached.!The!opposing!side!of!the!beam!monitored!by! sensor! pair! 647! showed! similar! attributes.! The! HMI! value! was! under! 0.3! as! the! load! was! approaching!225!kN,!although!as!the!load!was!increased!further,!approaching!the!cracking! load!of!275!kN!the!HMI!value!reached!0.59.!The!second!observed!crack!was!at!a!load!of!375! kN,! increasing! the! HMI! value! to! 0.74.! Overall! both! pairs! of! sensors! yielded! very! similar! results,! although! as! discovered! with! sensor! pairs! 647,! the! right! side! of! the! beam! shows! much!higher!HMI!values!and!thus!would!have!a!higher!combined!crack!width.!Based!on!the! results! of! the! HMI! value! and! the! threshold! developed! in! the! small! scale! experimental! program,!the!region!between!sensors!243!would!have!been!considered!cracked!at!a!load!of! 300!kN.!Similarly!the!region!between!sensor!pair!647!would!have!been!considered!cracked! at!a!load!of!250!kN.!Thus!the!results!of!the!piezo4system!provide!the!means!of!early!crack! detection;!providing!the!initiation!of!cracking!within!a!member!25!kN!prior!to!the!damage! becoming!visible!at!the!exterior.! Sensor! pairs! 142! and! 748! monitored! the! sections! directly! adjacent! the! supports.! These! sections!were!not!expected!to!crack,!but!rather!to!act!as!a!control!for!the!experiment.!The! HMI!was!calculated,!as!it!was!very!useful!in!validating!the!previously!established!benchmark! for! the! HMI.! As! the! support! sections! between! sensors! pairs! 142,! and! 748,! had! maximum! HMIs!of!0.42!and!0.38,!it!can!be!concluded!that!0.5!is!an!acceptable!limit!as!to!differentiate! between! a! section! where! cracking! is! visible! at! the! beam's! surface! exterior,! and! a! section! that!is!not!exhibiting!signs!of!cracking.! The! appearance! of! the! shear! cracks! in! beam! HS4L4M42! was! monitored! by! sensor! pairs! 943! and! 1046,! the! results! of! which! are! shown! in! Figure! 6.30.! The! 943! signal! path! was! visually! observed!to!be!intercepted!by!a!shear!crack!at!the!325!kN!load!step.!At!the!same!load!the! HMI!value!output!by!the!piezo4sensors!surpassed!the!cracking!threshold!of!0.5.!Sensor!pair! 1046!was!located!200!mm!closer!to!the!center!of!the!beam!than!sensor!pair!943.!This!shift!in! sensor!location!resulted!in!the!sensors!not!capturing!the!shear!crack,!but!rather,!the!sensors! pair,! captured! the! initiation! of! a! flexural4shear! crack.! The! crack! intercepted! the! signal! transmission!at!a!load!of!300!kN,!yielding!an!HMI!value!of!0.51.!These!results!indicate!that! 146!

the! sensor! pairs,! although! measuring! different! cracking! mechanisms! were! successful! in! capturing!the!inflicted!damage.!Both!piezo4sensor!pairs!yielded!similar!results,!and!had!they! been!the!primary!method!for!judging!the!member's!condition,!the!piezo4system!would!have! demonstrated!a!clear!warning!for!the!initiation!of!the!shear!crack.!

6.5.2.4 Strain,Readings,Using,Proposed,Model, The! small! scale! experimental! program! concluded! with! the! development! of! a! HMI4Strain! relationship! representing! the! internal! strain! experienced! by! a! member! during! the! un4 cracked! stages! of! the! member's! lifetime.! The! developed! model! was! applied! to! the! HMI! results!obtained!by!each!of!the!seven!signal!paths!that!monitored!the!flexural!behavior!of! beam!HS4L4M42.!The!results!of!the!fiber!optic!sensors,!where!available,!are!also!presented! parallel!to!the!piezo4sensor!results,!as!to!provide!a!means!for!comparison!of!the!accuracy!of! the!piezoceramic!system.!The!results!of!the!investigation!are!presented!in!Figure!6.32.!The! strain! readings! provided! by! the! piezo4sensors! can! also! be! compared! to! the! observed! cracking!pattern!of!the!beam!as!to!validate!the!cracking!limit!for!the!HMI.! The! most! critical! section! for! monitoring! the! beam's! strain! is! the! location! along! the! span,! directly!adjacent!to!the!support!location.!The!location!on!either!side!of!the!member!is!not! expected!to!crack!until!the!beam's!capacity!is!exceeded,!and!the!member!had!reached!the! failure!stage.!As!the!effective!shear!depth!of!the!specific!member!was!505!mm,!the!beam!is! not!expected!to!exhibit!any!cracking!up!to!a!distance!exceeding!505!mm!from!the!support! location.! Sensor! pairs! 142! on! the! left! side,! and! sensor! pair! 748! on! the! right! side! of! the! member!monitored!this!specific!region.!The!results!for!the!internal!strain!of!the!regions,!as! calculated!from!the!HMI!results,!is!presented!in!Figure!6.32a.!These!results!show!that!beam! HS4L4M42!experienced!a!much!higher!concentration!of!stress!at!the!left!support.!From!the! readings!obtained!between!sensor!pair!142,!the!beam!exceeded!the!110!4strain!limit!at!a! load! of! 450! kN,! suggesting! the! initiation! of! cracking.! Based! on! the! results! of! the! piezo4 sensors,! the! region! between! sensor! pair! 142! is! witnessed! to! have! a! final! strain! reading! of!

149!

200! 4strain! at! the! failure! load! of! 575! kN.! The! equivalent! crack! width! for! this! region! is! calculated! to! be! 0.036! mm,! suggesting! the! crack! is! too! small! to! be! visible! with! the! naked! eye,! and! thus! the! reason! for! it! not! being! visually! identified.! The! right! half! of! the! beam,! between!sensor!pair!748,!showed!a!slightly!less!severe!amount!of!damage.!The!strain!in!this! region!remains!within!the!un4cracked!limit!up!to!the!load!step!of!550!kN,!demonstrating!the! majority!of!strain!increase!in!between!the!450!and!575!kN!load!steps.!The!maximum!value! for!strain!reached!in!this!region!was!of!135!4strain.!Overall!the!sensor!pairs!monitoring!the! location!adjacent!to!the!supports!proved!to!be!rather!reliable!during!the!testing!period.!The! sensors!showed!minor!changes!in!the!strain!of!the!region!in!the!early!stages!of!loading,!and! demonstrated! a! clear! and! consistent! appearance! of! hairline! cracking! after! the! beam's! factored!resistant!moment!was!exceeded,!just!as!expected!of!the!member's!behavior.!

The! primary! difference! being! the! monitored! distance! of! each! system,! where! the! fiber! optic! sensor! is! monitoring! 200! mm! of! the! beam! the! piezo4ceramic! sensors! are! monitoring! 500! mm.! The! results! of! the! piezo4sensors! are! thus! expected! to! yield! slightly! higher!values!of!strain!than!the!fiber!optic!gauge,!although!the!two!systems!should!follow! the!same!trend,!just!as!illustrated!by!the!results!obtained.!! The! quarter4span! and! section! adjacent! to! the! mid4section! are! presented! in! Figure! 6.32b,! and! Figure! 6.32c.! Sensor! pair! 243! on! the! left! side! of! the! beam,! and! sensor! pair! 647! along! with!a!fiber!optic!cable!monitored!the!right!side!of!the!beam.!From!Figure!6.32b!the!results! of!the!three!reading!are!seen!to!be!in!good!agreement!with!one!another.!The!results!of!the! piezo4sensors!from!the!left!and!right!halves!of!the!beam!are!in!good!agreement!with!one! another,! where! the! right! side! of! the! beam! illustrates! a! slightly! higher! amount! of! damage.! The!section!adjacent!to!the!mid4section!monitored!by!sensor!pairs!344!and!546!demonstrate! a!similar!trend.!From!the!Load4Strain!graph!in!in!Figure!6.32c,!the!sensor!pairs!demonstrate! a!very!symmetric!behavior!for!beam!HS4L4M42,!although,!consistent!with!the!quarter4span,! the! strain! values! on! the! right! side! of! the! beam! are! seen! to! be! slightly! higher! than! those! captured!from!the!left.!The!graph!for!this!section!also!illustrates!a!very!similar!behavior!to! the!one!exhibited!by!the!mid4section!of!the!beam.!As!the!two!sections!undergo!the!same! value!of!moment,!the!two!sections!are!expected!to!have!very!similar!behaviors!during!the! loading!stages.!!! The! location! based! strain! readings! obtained! from! the! piezo4system! can! be! very! beneficial! for! the! non4destructive! evaluation! of! a! beam,! as! discovered! from! this! experimental! program.! The! piezo4sensors! are! very! effective! at! capturing! the! initiation! of! cracking! in! a! reinforced!concrete!member.!Using!this!knowledge,!along!with!the!limits!defining!a!cracked! member! (110! 4strain! and! HMI! exceeding! 0.27)! can! provide! a! means! of! establishing! the! various! stages! defined! by! the! code! that! a! member! undergoes! during! its! loading! program.! The!experimental!data!obtained!illustrated!a!clear!representation!of!the!two!loading!stages:! 151!

the! cracking! load,! and! the! ultimate! resistant! moment.! As! the! piezo4sensors! are! very! sensitive!to!the!appearance!of!cracking,!the!cracking!load!is!easily!captured!by!the!sensors! monitoring!the!location!of!maximum!moment!in!the!member,!in!this!case!sensor!pair!445.! The!calculated!cracking!load,!based!on!the!Canadian!code!previsions,!was!found!to!be!167.3! kN!for!the!specified!loading!set!up.!The!initiation!cracking!in!beam!HS4L4M42!was!observed! 17!kN!earlier!at!a!load!step!of!150!kN,!suggesting!the!member!cracked!before!this!load!step.! Based! on! the! obtained! results,! the! piezo4sensors! captured! cracking! at! the! mid4span! location,! as! well! as! the! locations! adjacent! to! the! mid4span! of! the! member,! at! the! 125! kN! load!step.!!! The!moment!when!the!beam!exceeded!its!ultimate!resistance!moment!was!captured!using! a!slightly!indirect!technique.!The!basic!behavior!of!a!reinforced!concrete!beam!dictates!that! a!beam!operating!in!its!design!limits!will!not!crack!within!a!distance,!equal!to!the!effective! shear!depth,!from!a!support.!Thus!a!crack!within!the!region!adjacent!to!the!support!would! imply!that!the!beam!has!exceeded!its!capacity,!or!the!ultimate!moment!of!resistance!of!the! member.!The!beam's!ultimate!carrying!capacity!was!calculated!to!be!569!kN!based!on!the! previsions!of!the!Canadian!code.!The!graph!illustrating!the!member's!behavior,!Figure!6.27,! yields! that! the! member's! ultimate! carrying! capacity! was,! in! fact,! exceeded! at! the! 550! kN.! Although,! no! visual! observation! of! the! cracking! at! the! support! location! was! captured,! the! piezo4system!demonstrated!that!the!left!side!of!the!beam!cracked!in!this!region!at!a!load!of! 550!kN!where!the!right!side!of!the!beam!exceeded!the!theoretical!cracking!limit!at!475!kN.! Thus,!the!piezo4system!was!found!to!be!effective!for!determining!of!two!of!the!four!stages! of! the! member's! loading! program.! The! continuing! objective! is! to! successfully! identify! the! load!step!at!which!beam!HS4L4M42!exceeded!its!serviceability!limit.!

The!left!side!of!the!beam!showed!very!similar!results.!The!propagation!of!the!shear!crack!on! this!side!was!visually!observed!to!intersect!the!signal!path!of!sensor!pair!943!at!a!load!of!325! kN,!and!detected!by!the!sensor!pair!at!250!kN.!The!sensor!pair!monitoring!the!shear!crack! on!the!left!half!of!member!HS4L4M42!also!illustrates!a!similar!trend!for!the!Load4Crack!Width! graph! presented! in! HS4L4M42! is! monitored! by! two! sensor! pairs.! The! results! of! the! piezo4sensors! consistently! point! to! two! sensor! pairs,! for! the! distinction! of! this! specific! load! step.! Sensor! pairs! 943! and! 243,! monitoring!the!left!half!of!beam!HS4L4M42,!both!differentiate!the!325!kN!load!step,!as!both! sensors!demonstrate!the!initiation!of!cracking!in!the!member!very!close!to!the!325!kN!load! step.!The!shear!crack!of!member!HS4L4M42!was!expected!to!initiate!at!a!load!of!300!kN,!as! calculated.! Thus! the! initiation! of! the! shear! crack! in! this! member! is! very! indicative! of! the! 158!

member!reaching!its!serviceability!limit!state,!in!this!particular!case.!Although!the!approach! for!determining!the!limit!state!is!indirect,!it!provides!a!good!means!of!establishing!a!warning! for! maintenance! engineers! to! assess! the! damage! induced! into! the! reinforced! concrete! member,! and! provides! the! required! rehabilitation! techniques! as! to! not! exceed! the! member's!serviceability!limit!state.!!

161!

Chapter!7!|!!!!!!!!!!

Conclusion!

The!proposed!system!proved!to!be!a!very!effective!tool!for!active!condition!assessment!of! reinforced! concrete! structures.! The! quick! responsiveness! and! high! signal! output! of! the! embedded! piezo4sensors,! along! with! their! durability! and! ease! of! integration! within! the! concrete!matrix!made!them!an!ideal!component!of!the!nondestructive!test!system.!! Throughout!the!preparation!of!the!test!specimens,!the!sensors!proved!to!be!very!durable.! The! high! heat! produced! during! the! curing! process! of! the! large4scale! specimens! had! no! effect! on! the! working! condition! of! these! piezo4sensors.! The! casting! process! did! not! cause! any!signs!of!damage!to!the!sensors.!The!piezoceramic!patches!used!in!the!fabrication!of!the! piezo4sensors! have! a! very! high! durability! to! high! temperature! exposure,! and! the! rugged! epoxy!encasing,!makes!them!ideal!for!structures!where!mass!concrete!is!used.!Although!the! sensors!were!designed!for!heavy!civil!structures!such!as!offshore!and!nuclear!containment!

163!

facilities,! they! are! not! limited! to! this! sort! of! structure.! The! senses! could! be! easily! implemented!into!any!reinforced!concrete!structure.!Theoretically,!the!operating!principle! of! the! sensors! would! allow! for! their! embedment! into! existing! structures,! although! the! investigation!was!not!verified!in!this!experimental!work.!

7.1

Findings

As! proposed! in! the! development! of! the! system,! the! piezo4sensors! were! very! effective! in! determining!the!initiation!of!cracking!within!a!concrete!member.!The!exceptional!sensitivity! of!the!system,!not!only!detected!the!initiation!of!cracking!within!a!member!it!also!proved!to! be!a!useful!tool!for!predictive!health!monitoring.!By!adopting!the!proposed!HMI!threshold! of!0.5,!the!system!provides!useful!information!as!to!when!a!member!is!expected!to!crack,! and! provides! an! early! warning! of! distress.! The! implementation! of! this! active! monitoring! system! for! real! time! continuous! recording! would! help! facilitate! the! maintenance! of! high! importance,!high!risk!facilities!by!providing!engineers!with!accurate,!up!to!date!information! about! the! building's! condition.! Using! the! information! provided! by! these! sensors,! maintenance!personal!could!prioritize,!and!effectively!assess!these!crucial!structures.!! The!developed!HMI4Crack!Width!model!for!the!system!proved!to!be!a!very!useful!tool!in!the! evaluation!of!the!reinforced!concrete!beams.!The!piezo4sensor!system!demonstrated!very! reliable! results,! when! compared! to! well! establish! system.! The! system! also! proved! to! be! more! reliable! in! the! evaluation! of! members! providing! a! complete! consensus! of! the! members'! behaviors! through! their! lifetimes.! The! piezoceramics! endured! the! casting! process,! and! continued! to! provide! results! up! to! the! failure! load! of! the! member.! The! embedded! piezo4sensors! also! demonstrated! the! means! of! establishing! a! beams! overall! condition.!The!various!limit!states!established!by!the!national!building!code!of!Canada!were! differentiable! from! the! signal! outputs! solely! making! the! system! a! very! useful! active! non4 destructive!testing!tool.! The! signal! outputs! of! the! piezo4system! were! successfully! processed! to! determine! the! development! of! concrete's! early! strength.! The! vibration! characteristic! of! a! section! was!

164!

successfully! related! to! the! development! of! strength! of! a! sample,! and! the! relationship! illustrated! by! Equation! 5.1! summarizes! this! result.! By! attaining! the! strength! of! a! concrete! sample! 24! hours! after! casting,! the! piezo4system! could! project! the! strength! gain! for! the! following!six!days!with!very!accurate!precision.!This!result!is!very!useful,!as!it!would!allow! for!the!use!of!the!same!array!of!sensors!that!provide!health!monitoring!information!about!a! sample,!during!the!construction!phases!of!the!building!to!prioritize!the!quality!control!of!the! cast! concrete.! The! system! can! then! provide! a! clear! representation! of! the! concrete's! strength!development!on!a!member4to4member!basis,!rather!than!the!global!method!relied! on!today.! The! signal! output! of! the! piezo4sensors! was! also! related! the! internal! concrete! strain! experienced!by!a!concrete!section.!The!relationship!was!achieved!through!the!investigation! of!small4scale!experimental!beams!equipped!with!strain!measuring!equipment.!The!output! signal! was! related! to! the! measurements! obtained! by! the! strain! measuring! equipment! to! establish!Equation!5.4.!This!equation!provides!a!means!of!relating!the!output!signal!of!the! piezo4sensors! (HMI)! to! the! crack! width! intersecting! the! signal! path.! The! relationship! is! summarized!in!Figure!6.15! The!relationship!obtained!between!the!piezo4sensor!signal,!and!the!crack!width!was!verified! using!a!couple!of!full4scale!experiment!beams,!that!were!equipped!with!Fiber!Bragg!Grating! fiber! optic! sensors.! A! comparison! between! the! two! systems! was! drawn,! as! to! verify! the! validity! for! the! piezo4system,! and! the! crack! width! relationship! determined! in! the! current! research.! Based! on! the! results! obtained! the! proposed! piezo4sensor! system! demonstrated! results!that!were!in!good!agreement!with!those!obtained!by!the!FBG!sensors.!The!reslts!of! the! full4scale! experimental! program! also! demonstrated! the! piezo4system's! location! based! capabilities.!The!strategic!distribution!of!piezo4sensors!inside!the!concrete!matrix!illustrated! one! of! the! key! advantages! of! using! the! piezo4system,! over! alternative! systems.! The! proposed!system!was!able!to!effectively!assess!the!condition!of!an!entire!member!based!on! the! assessment! of! signals! transferred! between! two! adjacent! sensors.! By! strategically! distributing! the! sensor! array! along! the! beams'! span,! multiple! sensor! combinations! can! be! used!to!effectively!monitor!the!structural!condition!of!a!member!on!the!entirety!of!its!span.! 165!

Unlike!alternative!embedded!non4destructive!systems,!the!proposed!piezo4ceramic!system! is! not! limited! to! a! specific! gauge! length,! yet! can! monitor! large! sections! of! a! reinforced! concrete!member!with!a!single!reading.!

7.2

MIRA 3D Tomographer

The! MIRA! tomograph! proves! to! be! an! effective! tool! for! the! non4destructive! evaluation! various! structural! components! that! is! available! on! the! market! today.! The! equipment! is! successful!in!determining!the!placement!condition!of!reinforcement!in!a!concrete!sample,! and!determining!the!punching!shear!failure!of!concrete!slabs.!Although!the!machine!has!a! specified! capability! of! reading! signals! to! a! depth! of! 2500! mm,! it! may! not! be! the! case! for! concrete! structures.! Material! inconsistencies! such! as! gradation! and! reinforcement! found! the! capability! the! MIRA! tomograph! to! only! about! 1600! mm! after! which! the! signal! is! completely! attenuated! and! there! is! very! minimal! reflections! returned! to! the! antenna! leading! to! inaccurate! and! irrelevant! reading! of! the! internal! structure.! The! equipment! was! also! found! to! be! successful! for! locating! signs! of! distress,! or! cracking,! in! a! concrete! beam,! although!it!is!not!successful!in!measuring!the!crack!widths!with!ease.!

7.3

Recommendations for Future Research

In!the!current!investigation,!the!piezo4sensors!have!been!proven!to!work!in!the!assessment! of!flexural!reinforced!concrete!members.!The!sensor!array's!was!proven!to!provide!accurate! information! about! the! initiation,! location,! and! magnitude! of! the! induced! damage! up! to! a! maximum! distance,! sensors4to4sensors,! of! 700! mm.! The! sensors! also! demonstrated! the! ability!of!transmitting!a!signal!up!to!a!maximum!distance!of!1600!mm,!although!having!no! reference! for! the! readings;! the! measurements! could! not! be! validated.! In! further! investigations,! the! sensor4to4sensor! distance! needs! to! be! increased,! and! the! effectiveness! of! crack! width! quantification! needs! to! be! verified.! A! full! investigation! needs! to! be! carried! out! as! to! determine! the! optimum! sensors4to4sensor! distances,! and! the! accuracy! of! the! piezo4sensors!system.!!
